DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Install base dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      cmake \
      git \
      ninja-build \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      binfmt-support \
      docker.io \
      docker-compose \
      curl \
      wget \
      unzip \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Configure QEMU for cross-arch emulation
  COPY --from=tonistiigi/binfmt:latest /usr/bin/qemu-* /usr/bin/
  RUN docker run --privileged --rm tonistiigi/binfmt --install all
  # Set up Docker-in-Docker
  RUN curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com | sh && \
      usermod -aG docker root
  # Install BuildKit for multi-platform builds
  RUN mkdir -p /etc/docker && \
      echo '{"features":{"buildkit":true}}' > /etc/docker/daemon.json
  # Clone repository and set up environment
  WORKDIR /repo
  COPY . .
  RUN chmod +x ./scripts/*.sh && \
      if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then pip install -r requirements.txt; fi && \
      if [ -f setup.py ]; then pip install -e .; fi
  # Configure entrypoint
  WORKDIR /repo
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Install base dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      cmake \
      git \
      ninja-build \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      qemu-user-static \
      qemu-system-arm \
      binfmt-support \
      curl \
      wget \
      unzip \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Configure QEMU without privileged operations
  COPY --from=tonistiigi/binfmt:latest /usr/bin/qemu-* /usr/bin/
  RUN update-binfmts --enable
  # Install Docker without privileged operations
  RUN curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com | sh
  # Configure BuildKit
  RUN mkdir -p /etc/docker && \
      echo '{"features":{"buildkit":true}}' > /etc/docker/daemon.json
  # Clone repository and set up environment
  WORKDIR /repo
  COPY . .
  RUN chmod +x ./scripts/*.sh && \
      if [ -f requirements.txt ]; then pip install -r requirements.txt; fi && \
      if [ -f setup.py ]; then pip install -e .; fi
  # Configure entrypoint
  WORKDIR /repo
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
